            window.onerror = function(messageOrEvent, source, lineNo, colNo, error) {
                try {
                    var errorMessage = '';
                    if(error) {
                        if(error.message && error.stack) {
                            errorMessage = (error.message + ' | ' + error.stack).substring(0,1000);
                        }
                        else if(error.message) {
                            errorMessage = error.message.substring(0,1000);
                        }
                        else if(error.stack) {
                            errorMessage = error.stack.substring(0,1000);
                        }
                    }
                    else if(messageOrEvent) {
                        errorMessage = messageOrEvent.substring(0,1000);
                    }
                    else {
                        throw 'Exception Details not available inside global error event handler';
                    }
                    logErrorsToServer(errorMessage);
                }
                catch(err) {
                    console.log('Error in Global Error Event Handler.' + err);
                }
            };
            var originalConsoleError = console.error;
            console.error = function error(errorMessage) {
                var message = 'console.error: ';
